< review>
Great local establishment serving steaks, seafood, and pasta.

Nice ambiance with an antique home feel. I love the painting of the octopus near the front.

We ordered the herb roasted chicken, sea bass, and calamari. All dishes were delicious, especially the sea bass. They also have a great kids menu and the grilled cheese with fries was also delicious as the adults stole samples from the little one.

For dessert, we had the Fonz's bar. A very healthy serving of two large caramel bars encrusted with nuts and topped with ice cream. This dessert is to die for.

Overall a great place and I would definitely return!</review>

Food is great; service was not. My party of 4 was seated for at least 20 minutes before finally being acknowledged by an employee (who we flagged down). We ordered our food and our drinks and had another long wait before any food came out. One of our dishes was incorrect and had to be sent back. There was a wait between every single dish for our table. Other tables seemingly received much better service than our own. Bottom line: this place has delicious food and good service unless you're not of Asian descent. Will probably stick to getting take out from now on.< /review>

< Name>
Eric Tam< /Name>
< Time>
1542845617322< /Time>
<rate>4<//rate>< review>
One of the few Chinese family style restaurants that don't use MSG in their food.. and this place proves that you don't need it for food to taste good.

This place is packed and for good reason. They have a 3 dish for $22.99 special that can feed a party of three. Or they have their standard offerings where you get an even bigger portion. Unfortunately I don't think they have the staff to handle this type of volume as the food came out pretty slow. On a Sunday night, we ordered our food at 6:30 PM and the first dish that came out was close to 7:00 PM, and the last dish came out around 8:30 PM.  Another problem with this restaurant, is there was a line of about five people deep waiting for the restroom.

Most of their dishes were spot on and memorable. Their soup of the day was on the mild side which is fine since there's no flavor enhancer. In fact, it was refreshing. They do make their Salty Fish and Chicken Fried Rice (there's a pungent smell so and the fish texture can be a turn off to some) very aromatic and with plenty of salty fish. The Chicken Curry had good flavor, but would've benefit from have more sauce. Garlic Green Bean was nice and crispy but would've prefer if they used less oil. Their Stir Fry Egg with Bitter Melon was well done, and so was their Fried Tofu. Their Sale and Pepper Spare Ribs was standard and would've been better if they cut the pieces of pork in smaller pieces.

This is one place worth trying but bring your patience.< /review>

<text>Fatally Flawed - Every visit, the cashier starts the interaction with "Phone number for your Ace rewards?" Not only are rewards clubs a privacy invasion, they are an attempt to manipulate my behavior, and most importantly (since I'll never join) this slows down the interaction of actually making a purchase and is an entirely unwelcome interruption to my task at hand.  If I say "I don't have one" they gleefully waste more of my time trying to get me sign up.  If I respond in the same manner as the cashier asked the original question - that is ignoring the goal of the person across from you such as telling them up front you're not interested - they act offended, like a street hustler who believes he has a right to trick you but just got found out!

Dear Ace manager... you should know that if I come in again and my time is yet again wasted with anything to do about your club I will file a BBB report on the issue. Need to satisfy Ace corporate morons pushing the program? Put a sign on the register for the stupid club and leave it at that!  I'll even provide a respectful sample cashier script... "Hi, did you find everything you needed today?" .... "thanks for coming in, we hope to see you again soon!" ...and leave it at that.  I would actually want to return if I were treated like that!  This is your opportunity to train your cashiers to respect others - they came to buy something, and that is all.  This behavior ruins an otherwise nice store... more games like this = more Amazon!     Love, Alex.

<Review>The lack of service is what killed this Buffalo Wild Wings for myself and several work friends.

We ( 8 people in total) arrived at 10 PM to a slightly packed house for a Tuesday night. After getting seating in the Bar Area we sat and conversed as we waited for menus and a server to come by for drink orders.

After 5 minutes of sitting and waiting we grabbed a menu and decided on which foods to order to help when the server came up to get drink orders. We figured help the server and the kitchen along at the same time instead of the time delay waiting for the drinks and ordering.

After a few more minutes, a friend decided to set a timer and see how long it would take for someone to come over and acknowledge us.

After 10 minutes on the timer ( at this point 17 or so minutes had passed) a server came up with menus and told us he would back to take our orders.

5 minutes later ( roughly 23 minutes since we had sat) and no server came by. We got up and left as a server came rushing up to "check on us".

Sorry BWW if this is the service to be expected, then sadly you will not see us here again.

Please be mindful people and call ahead to ensure it is not too busy otherwise what happened to us may happen to you< /Review><pics>None</pics>< resp>
